<script>
var msl_signedIn = false;
var lastfmid = "";
function toggleLoginScreen(showhide) {
	
	$('#headerScreen').toggle(showhide);
	$('#headerScreenLoginBox').toggle(showhide);
}


function mslSignIn(email, password) {
	$.ajax({
		url: "/ajax/signin",
	  	cache: false,
	  	data: 'email='+email+'&password='+password,
	  	type: "POST",
	  	dataType: "json",
	  	error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
			alert("Whoops\n\nThere was a network error. Please try again in a few moments.");
		},
		success: function(data, textStatus, xhr ){
			if (data.success) {
				document.location.href = '/mylist';
			} else {
				alert('Invalid email/password.  Please try again.');
			} 
		}
	});
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

$(document).ready(function(){
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-text').height() > 90) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-more').show();
	}
});

function toggleFinePrint() 
{
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-mask').hasClass('unmasked')) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').removeClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see more');
	} else {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').addClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see less');
	}
}
</script>

function executeMainSearch() {
	if($('#nav-search').val()!='Search Shows') {
		var nsf = document.getElementById("site-main-search-form");
		nsf.submit();
	}
}

function enableDatePicker()
{
	var dateToday = new Date();
	$.datepick.setDefaults({
			mandatory: true,
			rangeSelect: true,
			numberOfMonths: 1,
			showAnim: 'fadeIn',
			changeYear: false,
			changeMonth: false,
			duration: 200,
			minDate: dateToday,
			closeText: '<div alt="Close Date Picker" class="dpCloseBtn simplemodal-close" id="dpCloseBtn"></div>',
			dateFormat: 'mm/dd/yy',
			onClose: function(){
				$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
				$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
				//if($("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow").css('display')=='block') popDatePickerSimple();
			}
		});


	$('#when').datepick();
	$('#when').datepick('show');
	$('#when-datepicker-body').append( $('#datepick-div') );
}

$('#dpCloseBtn').live('click', hideDatePicker);

$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseover', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').show();});
$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseout', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').hide();});

	}
	*/
}

	$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
}

    FB.init({
      appId   : '269632832169',
      channelUrl  : '/public/xd_receiver.htm',
      status  : true, // check login status
      cookie  : true, // enable cookies to allow the server to access the session

	function update_fb_id(response){
	    if (response.authResponse) {
	    	//user is already logged in and connected
	      	fb_userId = response.authResponse.userID;
	    } else {
			//user is not connected to your app or logged out
			fb_userId = '';
	    }

	}

  FB.getLoginStatus(update_fb_id);
  FB.Event.subscribe('auth.statusChange', update_fb_id);
  };

<script>
var msl_signedIn = false;
var lastfmid = "";
function toggleLoginScreen(showhide) {
	
	$('#headerScreen').toggle(showhide);
	$('#headerScreenLoginBox').toggle(showhide);
}


function mslSignIn(email, password) {
	$.ajax({
		url: "/ajax/signin",
	  	cache: false,
	  	data: 'email='+email+'&password='+password,
	  	type: "POST",
	  	dataType: "json",
	  	error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
			alert("Whoops\n\nThere was a network error. Please try again in a few moments.");
		},
		success: function(data, textStatus, xhr ){
			if (data.success) {
				document.location.href = '/mylist';
			} else {
				alert('Invalid email/password.  Please try again.');
			} 
		}
	});
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

$(document).ready(function(){
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-text').height() > 90) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-more').show();
	}
});

function toggleFinePrint() 
{
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-mask').hasClass('unmasked')) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').removeClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see more');
	} else {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').addClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see less');
	}
}
</script>

function executeMainSearch() {
	if($('#nav-search').val()!='Search Shows') {
		var nsf = document.getElementById("site-main-search-form");
		nsf.submit();
	}
}

function enableDatePicker()
{
	var dateToday = new Date();
	$.datepick.setDefaults({
			mandatory: true,
			rangeSelect: true,
			numberOfMonths: 1,
			showAnim: 'fadeIn',
			changeYear: false,
			changeMonth: false,
			duration: 200,
			minDate: dateToday,
			closeText: '<div alt="Close Date Picker" class="dpCloseBtn simplemodal-close" id="dpCloseBtn"></div>',
			dateFormat: 'mm/dd/yy',
			onClose: function(){
				$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
				$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
				//if($("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow").css('display')=='block') popDatePickerSimple();
			}
		});


	$('#when').datepick();
	$('#when').datepick('show');
	$('#when-datepicker-body').append( $('#datepick-div') );
}

$('#dpCloseBtn').live('click', hideDatePicker);

$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseover', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').show();});
$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseout', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').hide();});

}

    FB.init({
      appId   : '269632832169',

      status  : true, // check login status
      cookie  : true, // enable cookies to allow the server to access the session

	function update_fb_id(response){
	    if (response.authResponse) {
	    	//user is already logged in and connected
	      	fb_userId = response.authResponse.userID;
	    } else {
			//user is not connected to your app or logged out
			fb_userId = '';
	    }

	}

  FB.Event.subscribe('auth.statusChange', update_fb_id);
  };

<script>
var msl_signedIn = false;
var lastfmid = "";
function toggleLoginScreen(showhide) {
	
	$('#headerScreen').toggle(showhide);
	$('#headerScreenLoginBox').toggle(showhide);
}


function mslSignIn(email, password) {
	$.ajax({
		url: "/ajax/signin",
	  	cache: false,
	  	data: 'email='+email+'&password='+password,
	  	type: "POST",
	  	dataType: "json",
	  	error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
			alert("Whoops\n\nThere was a network error. Please try again in a few moments.");
		},
		success: function(data, textStatus, xhr ){
			if (data.success) {
				document.location.href = '/mylist';
			} else {
				alert('Invalid email/password.  Please try again.');
			} 
		}
	});
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

$(document).ready(function(){
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-text').height() > 90) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-more').show();
	}
});

function toggleFinePrint() 
{
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-mask').hasClass('unmasked')) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').removeClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see more');
	} else {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').addClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see less');
	}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" src="/min/?f=public/jquery/jquery.datepick.js"></script>
<!-- <script src="http://static.ak.connect.facebook.com/js/api_lib/v0.4/FeatureLoader.js.php/en_US" type="text/javascript"></script> -->
<script type='text/javascript'>
//<![CDATA[

function executeMainSearch() {
	if($('#nav-search').val()!='Search Shows') {
		var nsf = document.getElementById("site-main-search-form");
		nsf.submit();
	}
}

function enableDatePicker()
{
	var dateToday = new Date();
	$.datepick.setDefaults({
			mandatory: true,
			rangeSelect: true,
			numberOfMonths: 1,
			showAnim: 'fadeIn',
			changeYear: false,
			changeMonth: false,
			duration: 200,
			minDate: dateToday,
			closeText: '<div alt="Close Date Picker" class="dpCloseBtn simplemodal-close" id="dpCloseBtn"></div>',
			dateFormat: 'mm/dd/yy',
			onClose: function(){
				$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
				$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
				//if($("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow").css('display')=='block') popDatePickerSimple();
			}
		});


	$('#when').datepick();
	$('#when').datepick('show');
	$('#when-datepicker-body').append( $('#datepick-div') );
}

$('#dpCloseBtn').live('click', hideDatePicker);

$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseover', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').show();});

function hideDatePicker(){ 
	$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
	$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
}

<script>

function checkEnterLogin(e) {
	if(e.keyCode == 13){
		mslSignIn($('#login_email_input').val(), $('#login_password_input').val())
	}
}

$('#login_password_input').keydown(checkEnterLogin);


var fb_userId;
var fb_init_loaded = false;
var fb_onload_msl_function = function(){};

  fb_userId = '';

  window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
    FB.init({
      appId   : '269632832169',
      channelUrl  : '/public/xd_receiver.htm',
      status  : true, // check login status
      cookie  : true, // enable cookies to allow the server to access the session
      xfbml   : true, // parse XFBML
      oauth   : true
    });

    fb_init_loaded = true;
    fb_onload_msl_function();

	function update_fb_id(response){
	    if (response.authResponse) {
	    	//user is already logged in and connected
	      	fb_userId = response.authResponse.userID;
	    } else {
			//user is not connected to your app or logged out
			fb_userId = '';
	    }
	    
	    //alert(fb_userId);
	}

  // run once with current status and whenever the status changes
  FB.getLoginStatus(update_fb_id);
  FB.Event.subscribe('auth.statusChange', update_fb_id);
  };

  (function() {
  var e = document.createElement('script');
    e.src = document.location.protocol + '//connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js';
    e.async = true;
    document.getElementById('fb-root').appendChild(e);
  }());
</script>

<script>
var msl_signedIn = false;
var lastfmid = "";
function toggleLoginScreen(showhide) {
	
	$('#headerScreen').toggle(showhide);
	$('#headerScreenLoginBox').toggle(showhide);
}


function mslSignIn(email, password) {
	$.ajax({
		url: "/ajax/signin",
	  	cache: false,
	  	data: 'email='+email+'&password='+password,
	  	type: "POST",
	  	dataType: "json",
	  	error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
			alert("Whoops\n\nThere was a network error. Please try again in a few moments.");
		},
		success: function(data, textStatus, xhr ){
			if (data.success) {
				document.location.href = '/mylist';
			} else {
				alert('Invalid email/password.  Please try again.');
			} 
		}
	});
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

$(document).ready(function(){
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-text').height() > 90) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-more').show();
	}
});

function toggleFinePrint() 
{
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-mask').hasClass('unmasked')) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').removeClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see more');
	} else {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').addClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see less');
	}
}
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
//<![CDATA[

function executeMainSearch() {
	if($('#nav-search').val()!='Search Shows') {
		var nsf = document.getElementById("site-main-search-form");
		nsf.submit();
	}
}

function enableDatePicker()
{
	var dateToday = new Date();
	$.datepick.setDefaults({
			mandatory: true,
			rangeSelect: true,
			numberOfMonths: 1,
			showAnim: 'fadeIn',
			changeYear: false,
			changeMonth: false,
			duration: 200,
			minDate: dateToday,
			closeText: '<div alt="Close Date Picker" class="dpCloseBtn simplemodal-close" id="dpCloseBtn"></div>',
			dateFormat: 'mm/dd/yy',
			onClose: function(){
				$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
				$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
				//if($("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow").css('display')=='block') popDatePickerSimple();
			}
		});


	$('#when').datepick();
	$('#when').datepick('show');
	$('#when-datepicker-body').append( $('#datepick-div') );
}

$('#dpCloseBtn').live('click', hideDatePicker);

$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseover', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').show();});
$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseout', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').hide();});

function showDatePicker(){ 

	$('#when-datepicker-box').show();
	
	$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: hideDatePicker();');

	var m = $("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow");	
	

	/*
	if( m.css('display')=='block' ){	
		popDatePickerSimple();
	}
	*/
}
function hideDatePicker(){ 
	$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
	$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
}

function simpleWhenPicker(date_token)
{

	$('#when').val(date_token);
	//if($("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow").css('display')=='block') popDatePickerSimple();
}

/*
function popDatePickerSimple()
{
	var t = document.getElementById("when-container");
	
	var m = $("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow");
	$(t).append(m);
	
	var m_display = (m.css('display')=='block') ? 'none' : 'block';


	m.css('left',1);
	m.css('top',27);

	m.css('display',m_display);

}
*/

function submitDatePicker() {
	jQuery.datepick._hideDatepick();
	$('#dateSearchForm').submit();
}

$(document).ready(function(){

	$('#header').click(function(event) {toggleLoginScreen(false);});
	$('#headerScreen').click(function(event) {toggleLoginScreen(false);});
	$('#headerScreenLoginBox').click(function(event) {event.stopPropagation();});
		
		enableDatePicker();
	});

	function update_fb_id(response){
	    if (response.authResponse) {
	    	//user is already logged in and connected
	      	fb_userId = response.authResponse.userID;
	    } else {

	    }

	}

  FB.getLoginStatus(update_fb_id);
  FB.Event.subscribe('auth.statusChange', update_fb_id);
  };

<script>
var msl_signedIn = false;
var lastfmid = "";
function toggleLoginScreen(showhide) {
	
	$('#headerScreen').toggle(showhide);
	$('#headerScreenLoginBox').toggle(showhide);
}


function mslSignIn(email, password) {
	$.ajax({
		url: "/ajax/signin",
	  	cache: false,
	  	data: 'email='+email+'&password='+password,
	  	type: "POST",
	  	dataType: "json",
	  	error: function(XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown){
			alert("Whoops\n\nThere was a network error. Please try again in a few moments.");
		},
		success: function(data, textStatus, xhr ){
			if (data.success) {
				document.location.href = '/mylist';
			} else {
				alert('Invalid email/password.  Please try again.');
			} 
		}
	});
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

$(document).ready(function(){
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-text').height() > 90) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-more').show();
	}
});

function toggleFinePrint() 
{
	if ($('#venue-fine-print-mask').hasClass('unmasked')) {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').removeClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see more');
	} else {
		$('#venue-fine-print-mask').addClass('unmasked');
		$('#venue-fine-print-more a').text('see less');
	}
}
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
//<![CDATA[

function executeMainSearch() {
	if($('#nav-search').val()!='Search Shows') {
		var nsf = document.getElementById("site-main-search-form");
		nsf.submit();
	}
}

function enableDatePicker()
{
	var dateToday = new Date();
	$.datepick.setDefaults({
			mandatory: true,
			rangeSelect: true,
			numberOfMonths: 1,
			showAnim: 'fadeIn',
			changeYear: false,
			changeMonth: false,
			duration: 200,
			minDate: dateToday,
			closeText: '<div alt="Close Date Picker" class="dpCloseBtn simplemodal-close" id="dpCloseBtn"></div>',
			dateFormat: 'mm/dd/yy',
			onClose: function(){
				$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
				$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
				//if($("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow").css('display')=='block') popDatePickerSimple();
			}
		});


	$('#when').datepick();
	$('#when').datepick('show');
	$('#when-datepicker-body').append( $('#datepick-div') );
}

$('#dpCloseBtn').live('click', hideDatePicker);

$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseover', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').show();});
$('.mslsync-random-buzzed').live('mouseout', function() {$(this).find('.mslsync-random-buzzed-hover').hide();});

function showDatePicker(){ 

	$('#when-datepicker-box').show();
	
	$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: hideDatePicker();');

	var m = $("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow");	
	

	/*
	if( m.css('display')=='block' ){	
		popDatePickerSimple();
	}
	*/
}
function hideDatePicker(){ 
	$('#when-datepicker-box').hide();
	$('#searchCalendarIconAction').attr('href','javascript: showDatePicker();');
}

function simpleWhenPicker(date_token)
{

	$('#when').val(date_token);
	//if($("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow").css('display')=='block') popDatePickerSimple();
}

/*
function popDatePickerSimple()
{
	var t = document.getElementById("when-container");
	
	var m = $("#sml-dropdown-concertSearchArrow");
	$(t).append(m);
	
	var m_display = (m.css('display')=='block') ? 'none' : 'block';


	m.css('left',1);
	m.css('top',27);

	m.css('display',m_display);

}
*/

function submitDatePicker() {
	jQuery.datepick._hideDatepick();
	$('#dateSearchForm').submit();
}

$(document).ready(function(){

	$('#header').click(function(event) {toggleLoginScreen(false);});
	$('#headerScreen').click(function(event) {toggleLoginScreen(false);});
	$('#headerScreenLoginBox').click(function(event) {event.stopPropagation();});
		
		enableDatePicker();
	});

<script>
	$('#feedback_submit').click(function(event){
		event.preventDefault();

		$('#feedbackModalRightSubmit').show();
		$('#feedbackModalRightCorrect').hide();
	});
	$('#feedback_correct').click(function(event){
		event.preventDefault();

		$('#feedbackModalRightSubmit').hide();
		$('#feedbackModalRightCorrect').show();
	});
</script>

<script>

function checkEnterLogin(e) {
	if(e.keyCode == 13){
		mslSignIn($('#login_email_input').val(), $('#login_password_input').val())
	}
}

$('#login_password_input').keydown(checkEnterLogin);


var fb_userId;
var fb_init_loaded = false;
var fb_onload_msl_function = function(){};

  fb_userId = '';

  window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
    FB.init({
      appId   : '269632832169',
      channelUrl  : '/public/xd_receiver.htm',
      status  : true, // check login status
      cookie  : true, // enable cookies to allow the server to access the session
      xfbml   : true, // parse XFBML
      oauth   : true
    });

    fb_init_loaded = true;
    fb_onload_msl_function();

	function update_fb_id(response){
	    if (response.authResponse) {
	    	//user is already logged in and connected
	      	fb_userId = response.authResponse.userID;
	    } else {
			//user is not connected to your app or logged out
			fb_userId = '';
	    }
	    
	    //alert(fb_userId);
	}

  // run once with current status and whenever the status changes
  FB.getLoginStatus(update_fb_id);
  FB.Event.subscribe('auth.statusChange', update_fb_id);
  };

  (function() {
  var e = document.createElement('script');
    e.src = document.location.protocol + '//connect.facebook.net/en_US/all.js';
    e.async = true;
    document.getElementById('fb-root').appendChild(e);
  }());
</script>
